[18:23] <freakynl> so your dns client adds the search domain, fritz.box in this case, making the request whatever.fritz.box
[18:23] <freakynl> your router (a fritz box apparently :)) has a dns file stating *.fritz.box points to that IP

=== daftykin1 is now known as daftykins
